_1_o" href="#" role="button"><i class="lock img sp_8u5rsk sx_f7667f"></i></a></div></div></div><div class="aboveUnitContent"><div class="userContentWrapper"><div class="_wk"><span class="userContent"><div id="id_521d096de70e63844674188" class="text_exposed_root">Jack Ingram - STEAM Magazine Interview<br /> Did you catch Jack Ingram on Day Jobs? It’s a Great American Country (GAC) series that takes country stars back “before they made it big” and has them experience a day’s work in either a job they had h<span class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span class="text_exposed_show">eld or a job they always wanted to do. While growing up Jack’s father had a ’55 t-bird, and later a ’56 t-bird, however, he didn’t work on them, something Jack had always wanted to do.  So he took the job and learned a few tricks of the auto trade from Greening Auto in Nashville. <br /> STEAM - Just about everyone who knows Jack, knows he is a great songwriter and puts on a great show. You will be headlining at Sharkeys Port Aransas Summerfest Concert Series on Saturday August 31. How often do you get a chance to play here? <br /> Jack - We get to South Texas at least once or twice a year; we love playing there and always have a great time. <br /> STEAM - You have been very busy! I recently saw you on Texas Music Scene as the Whataburger performance of the week and that was an awesome version of &quot;Love You&quot;. But I have to ask about your plane show. You partnered up with the Boot Campaign and Southwest Airlines to perform Live at 35,000 Feet on a flight from Austin to Dallas. What was that like?<br /> Jack - It was great and one of those memorable experiences! I’ve always wanted to break out my guitar and play and I’ve been asked on flights to play, but I had just never done it. I’m glad I was given that opportunity to and to share it with Jeremy Smith (a returning vet) and his fiancée.<br /> STEAM - All of your fans are anxiously waiting for a new album; when can we expect your next project? <br /> Jack - I’ve been working on it for about 6 or 8 months and it’s about half way done. I’m hoping to release it in 2013. <br /> STEAM - I know you are about to go on stage somewhere so I’ll wish you a great show! Thanks for taking a few minutes to talk with me. See you in Port Aransas.<br /> For up-to-date show information and watch for that new album check out Jack Ingram at <a href="http://www.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.jackingram.net&amp;h=aAQGYJ3eC&amp;s=1" rel="nofollow nofollow" target="_blank" onmouseover="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/www.jackingram.net\\/&quot;);" onclick="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/www.facebook.com\\/l.php?u=http\\u00253A\\u00252F\\u00252Fwww.jackingram.net&amp;h=aAQGYJ3eC&amp;s=1&quot;);">www.jackingram.net</a></span><span class="text_exposed_hide"><span class="text_exposed_link"><a onclick="var parent = Parent.byClass(this, &quot;text_exposed_root&quot;); if (parent &amp;&amp; parent.getAttribute(&quot;id&quot;) == &quot;id_521d096de70e63844674188&quot;) &#123; CSS.addClass(parent, &quot;text_exposed&quot;); Arbiter.inform(&quot;reflow&quot;); &#125;" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;e&quot;&#125;">See More</a></span></span></div></span></div></div></div><div class="photoUnit clearfix"><div class="_53s uiScaledThumb photo photoWidth1" data-gt="&#123;&quot;fbid&quot;:&quot;513979375361563&quot;&#125;" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;E&quot;&#125;"><a class="_6i9" href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=513979375361563&amp;set=a.243649815727855.56339.243643805728456&amp;type=1&amp;relevant_count=1" rel="theater" ajaxify="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=513979375361563&amp;set=a.243649815727855.56339.243643805728456&amp;type=1&amp;relevant_count=1&amp;src=https%3A%2F%2Ffbcdn-sphotos-h-a.akamaihd.net%2Fhphotos-ak-ash4%2F1277495_513979375361563_1552057340_o.jpg&amp;smallsrc=https%3A%2F%2Fsphotos-b.xx.fbcdn.net%2Fhphotos-ash4%2F1186025_513979375361563_1552057340_n.jpg&amp;size=1027%2C1022&amp;theater&amp;source=9"><div class="uiScaledImageContainer photoWrap"><img class="img" src="https://sphotos-b.xx.fbcdn.net/hphotos-ash4/p480x480/1186025_513979375361563_1552057340_n.jpg" style="left:0px;" alt="Photo: Jack Ingram - STEAM Magazine Interview
Did you catch Jack Ingram on Day Jobs? It&#x2019;s a Great American Country (GAC) series that takes country stars back &#x201c;before they made it big&#x201d; and has them experience a day&#x2019;s work in either a job they had held or a job they always wanted to do. While growing up Jack&#x2019;s father had a &#x2019;55 t-bird, and later a &#x2019;56 t-bird, however, he didn&#x2019;t work on them, something Jack had always wanted to do.  So he took the job and learned a few tricks of the auto trade from Greening Auto in Nashville. 
STEAM - Just about everyone who knows Jack, knows he is a great songwriter and puts on a great show. You will be headlining at Sharkeys Port Aransas Summerfest Concert Series on Saturday August 31. How often do you get a chance to play here? 
Jack - We get to South Texas at least once or twice a year; we love playing there and always have a great time. 
STEAM - You have been very busy! I recently saw you on Texas Music Scene as the Whataburger performance of the week and that was an awesome version of &quot;Love You&quot;. But I have to ask about your plane show. You partnered up with the Boot Campaign and Southwest Airlines to perform Live at 35,000 Feet on a flight from Austin to Dallas. What was that like?
Jack - It was great and one of those memorable experiences! I&#x2019;ve always wanted to break out my guitar and play and I&#x2019;ve been asked on flights to play, but I had just never done it. I&#x2019;m glad I was given that opportunity to and to share it with Jeremy Smith (a returning vet) and his fianc&#xe9;e.
STEAM - All of your fans are anxiously waiting for a new album; when can we expect your next project? 
Jack - I&#x2019;ve been working on it for about 6 or 8 months and it&#x2019;s about half way done. I&#x2019;m hoping to release it in 2013. 
STEAM - I know you are about to go on stage somewhere so I&#x2019;ll wish you a great show! Thanks for taking a few minutes to talk with me. See you in Port Aransas.
For up-to-date show information and watch for that new album check out Jack Ingram at www.jackingram.net" width="405" height="403" /></div></a></div></div></div><div class="fbTimelineUFI
